# HUNTER — доаудит round 2 · ПРЕДВАРИТЕЛЬНЫЙ отчёт

> ⚠️ **СТАТУС: ПРЕДВАРИТЕЛЬНЫЙ.** Аудит завершён по всем 74 файлам. Адверсариальная верификация закрыта по **чанкам 1–3 полностью + чанк 4 частично**; находки чанков 4–8 (73 шт.) **НЕ верифицированы** — верификаторы упали по session-limit (сброс токенов 4am PT). Список неверифицированного — в аппендиксе внизу; дожать резюмом (тот же runId `wf_b6b9108d-634`, только в этой сессии) или отдельным verify-only проходом после 4am.

Read-only доаудит модулей, не пройденных пофайлово в round 1. Truth priority: **метод каналов > согласованность кода > статьи**. Классы: **A** метод / **B** нет-методной-опоры / **C** внутреннее противоречие / **D** доставка. Severity: **P0** искажает сигнал/статистику / **P1** контракт/лейбл / **P2** техдолг/мёртвый код.

Верификация адверсариальная. **CONFIRMED** — воспроизведено → номер G-31+. **PLAUSIBLE (гипотеза)** — правдоподобно, репро нет. **НЕ ВЕРИФИЦИРОВАНО** — аудит есть, верификатор не отработал (session limit, резюм после 4am PT). REFUTED отсеяны.

## Чанк 1 — runtime/cycle

### runtime/cycle/_cycle_ledger.py
- **Назначение:** Records an outcome-ledger row (and, when not delivered, a shadow-reject row) for a signal at the emit boundary; extracted from _cycle_tick.
- **Методная опора:** No direct method basis — backend outcome/telemetry accounting, not a signal-generation feature. Supports later calibration of delivered vs rejected outcomes.
- **G-32** ✅ — **`if not delivered:` shadow-reject branch is unreachable; the entire track/shadow.py reject log is orphaned (never written, never read)**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/cycle/_cycle_ledger.py:35-49` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** record_outcome_ledger has exactly ONE caller: emitter.py:58-66 (_record_deep_outcome), which hard-codes `delivered=True, blockers=[]` and always passes an explicit `event=`. So `if not delivered:` at line 35 is never True → lines 35-49 never execute. The imports at lines 36-39 (append_shadow_reject, shadow_record_from_delivery) are the ONLY importers of hunt_core/track/shadow.py anywhere: `grep -rn 'from hunt_core.track.shadow\|hunt_shadow_rejects\|SHADOW_JSONL' hunt_core research scripts tests` returns only shadow.py's own definitions and this dead branch. hunt_shadow_rejects.jsonl (shadow.py:11) is therefore never produced and no code reads it. shadow.py's docstring claims a 'Unified shadow log for delivery rejects and no-signal paths' but neither path is wired. The function's `event='blocked'` default, `delivered=False` default, `setup=None` default and `blockers` param exist only for this non-existent reject call site.
  - **Репро:** grep for `record_outcome_ledger(` shows the sole caller emitter.py:58 passes delivered=True; run the watcher and inspect data/ — hunt_shadow_rejects.jsonl is never created. A unit test asserting append_shadow_reject is called on any live path fails: no reachable code path invokes it.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either (a) remove the unreachable branch (lines 35-49) plus the now-orphaned hunt_core/track/shadow.py module and the reject-only parameter defaults; or (b) if reject-shadow logging is actually wanted, add the missing blocked/rejected call site (out-of-scope new wiring). Minimal on existing data = delete lines 35-49 and shadow.py.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text — this is backend telemetry. The reject-outcome shadow ledger that later reject-rate calibration would consume is simply never populated; delivered-outcome recording (line 34) is unaffected.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — Reproduced the finding exactly at hunt_core/runtime/cycle/_cycle_ledger.py:35-49. record_outcome_ledger has exactly one caller: emitter.py:58 (_record_deep_outcome), which hard-codes delivered=True and blockers=[]. _record_deep_outcome in turn has a single call site (emitter.py:49) with no path that sets delivered=False. Therefore `if not delivered:` at line 35 is never True and lines 35-49 (the only importers of hunt_core.track.shadow) never run. grep for `from hunt_core.track.shadow|append_shadow_reject|shadow_record_from_delivery|hunt_shadow_rejects|SHADOW_JSONL` across hunt_core/research/s …[обрезано]
- ❌ *REFUTED* — **LOG.warning uses %-style positional formatting instead of structlog key=value idiom**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/cycle/_cycle_ledger.py:51-57` · класс D / library / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 51-57 calls `LOG.warning("outcome_ledger_failed | symbol=%s direction=%s event=%s error=%s", symbol, direction, event, exc)`. Placeholder count (4 %s) matches arg count (4), and modern structlog's FilteringBoundLogger does `event % args`, so output renders correctly — this is NOT a functional bug. But the project logging skill mandates structured key=value pairs (`LOG.warning("outcome_ledger_failed", symbol=symbol, direction=direction, event=event, error=str(exc))`), so the message renders as an un-parseable pre-formatted string rather than structured fields.
  - **Репро:** No failing behaviour; grep the file for the %-format string. Cosmetic/log-parsing only.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Rewrite as key=value: `LOG.warning("outcome_ledger_failed", symbol=symbol, direction=direction, event=event, error=str(exc))`.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to Telegram output; only the shape of an internal warning log line.
  - **Вердикт:** REFUTED — The code at _cycle_ledger.py:51-57 does literally use `LOG.warning("outcome_ledger_failed | symbol=%s direction=%s event=%s error=%s", symbol, direction, event, exc)` as described, and the auditor concedes there is no functional impact (placeholder/arg counts match; structlog renders it correctly). The finding is refuted as a defect on three grounds: (1) The cited logging skill (.opencode/skills/logging/SKILL.md) does NOT forbid %-style positional formatting — its single explicit BAD example is an f-string (`LOG.info(f"symbol_fetched {symbol}")`), and this code correctly avoids f-strings. The  …[обрезано]

But the three error-row builders here hardcode the batch param `tier`: line 255 (timeout), line 264 (IncompleteReadError), and _settle_snapshot_results line 80 (unhandled exc, called with tier=tier at line 281). tier_by_symbol is genuinely populated per-symbol (capacity.py:184 → _cycle_loop.py:854 passes it), so a symbol assigned 'fast' via tier_by_symbol that times out inside a 'full' batch emits an error row tagged snapshot_tier='full'. sym_tier=_tier_for(sym) is already computed at line 211 but not used in the except branches.
  - **Репро:** Call run_tick with tier='full' and tier_by_symbol={'XUSDT':'fast'}; force snapshot_symbol('XUSDT') to raise TimeoutError. Resulting row['snapshot_tier']=='full' though the symbol was snapshotted 'fast'.
  - **Мин. фикс:** In the timeout/IncompleteReadError handlers use `"snapshot_tier": sym_tier`; for _settle_snapshot_results pass the per-symbol tier (or accept a tier lookup) rather than the single batch `tier`.

  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — Code matches the claim exactly. The success path diverges: tick_assembly.py:834 stamps snapshot_tier from its per-symbol tier arg, which run_tick passes as sym_tier at line 237 — so a healthy fast-tier symbol row is labeled "fast". ## Чанк 2 — runtime

### runtime/analyst_assembly.py
- **Назначение:** Module-1 "deep" tick orchestrator: assembles a full Prizrak structure-first snapshot per pinned symbol, runs it through the lifecycle spine, and emits per-setup_kind Telegram messages.
- **Методная опора:** Implements the Prizrak decision-authority delivery plane.
- **G-46** ✅ — **Phantom key rr_base_label: read on the activation message, never written anywhere**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/analyst_assembly.py:381` · класс D / dead-code / **P2**

### runtime/signals_report.py
- **Назначение:** Builds the /signals Telegram report: watchlist snapshot + active-tracker position blocks (PnL, TP progress, re-alert status, rollup summary).

- **G-42** ✅ — **"✅ Re-alert сейчас прошёл бы" is unreachable — primary.ok is structurally always False, and summary count uses a different gate**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/signals_report.py:308` · класс C / logic / **P1**

So `primary` is either None or a GateResult with ok==False. Therefore `primary is not None and primary.ok` == (False) always → line 309 is dead. Worse: when the setup IS re-alertable (impulse_confirmed truthy), collect_report_blockers returns [] → primary=None and extra=[] → the elif at 310 (realert_blockers) is also empty → the block prints NO re-alert line at all. Net: the summary can say "N re-alert" while not a single position block shows the re-alert-passed line.

  - **Мин. фикс:** Replace the condition at line 308 with a gate that can be True, e.g. `if primary is None and evaluate_alert_gate(setup, direction=direction, symbol=sym, lifecycle=lc, row=row).ok:` (evaluate_alert_gate is already imported and used at line 209), so a confirmed setup renders the positive line and unconfirmed falls through to the blocker elif.

After: the block shows "✅ Re-alert сейчас прошёл бы" for exactly the positions the summary counts.

### runtime/symbol_probe.py
- **Назначение:** On-demand /signal (and /signals catalog, delivery, deep) symbol probe: builds a full hunt row via an isolated REST client, enriches pinned anchors with cross-exchange + maps, and formats the Telegram reply.

The other call site of the same build_map_bundle, tick_assembly.py:1014, does the OPPOSITE with an explicit corrective comment (1010-1013): "`global_ls_ratio` must be the GLOBAL account ratio; top-trader L/S is a different population. Prefer the global series and fall back to top only when it is missing (was the other way round, so forward-zone long_share reflected top accounts while calling itself global)." That reordering fix landed in tick_assembly but NOT here. Downstream, maps/liquidation.py:309-310 does `long_share = global_ls_ratio/(1.0+global_ls_ratio)` — the value seeds the long/short split of every liquidation cluster. top_ls_1h (top_position_ls_ratio) and global_ls_1h (global_ls_ratio) are distinct Binance populations (producers: features/snapshot.py:868/870). So for a pinned anchor (BTC/ETH/XAU/XAG) the /signal maps block splits liquidation clusters by top-trader positioning while the passive scanner splits the SAME symbol by global accounts. Note symbol_probe also omits …[обрезано]

  - **Мин. фикс:** Mirror tick_assembly.py:1014/1025: change line 318 to `global_ls_ratio=float(market.get("global_ls_1h") or market.get("top_ls_1h") or 0) or None`, and add `top_ls_ratio=float(market.get("top_ls_1h") or 0) or None` to the build_map_bundle call so ls_for_fuel stays consistent with the scanner. - **G-61** ✅ — **Depth-1 /signal queue can silently drop a queued request — 'runs automatically' promise unmet when it arrives during the queued probe**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/telegram_commands.py:204-214` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** The drain is a one-shot `if pending is not None` (205-214) that spawns _run_signal_probe DIRECTLY as a task and never re-checks _pending_signal afterward. _run_signal_probe (216) does not touch the queue. So: R1 runs inline (holds lock); R2 arrives during R1 -> sets _pending_signal, told 'runs automatically сразу после'; R1 finishes -> drains R2 into a fire-and-forget task (209); R3 arrives WHILE the R2 task holds the lock -> _handle_signal sees lock locked -> sets _pending_signal=R3, sends the same 'runs automatically' reply; R2 task ends via _run_signal_probe -> nobody drains R3. R3 is never executed until an unrelated future R4 arrives when the lock is free (whose _handle_signal drains it). If no R4 ever comes, R3 is lost despite the user being promised auto-execution. Only the inline path (204) drains; the spawned-task path (209) is a dead end.
  - **Репро:** Fire three /signal in quick succession (each probe ~seconds). Msg1 runs; msg2 replies 'queued'; msg3 sent while msg2's queued probe is running replies 'queued, runs automatically' but its probe never fires and no further reply is ever produced.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Replace the one-shot `if pending` with a drain loop inside _handle_signal's post-probe section: `while (pending := self._pending_signal) is not None: self._pending_signal = None; await self._run_signal_probe(*pending)` (runs sequentially off the poll loop, so awaiting inline is fine). This keeps the depth-1 latest-wins semantics while guaranteeing the last queued request always runs.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** A queued /signal that today is silently dropped will now actually be answered, matching the 'выполнится автоматически сразу после' promise the bot already prints.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — Code at hunt_core/runtime/telegram_commands.py:204-214 matches the finding. grep confirms _pending_signal is read/drained ONLY at lines 205-206, inside the inline branch of _handle_signal — there is no background loop and no other consumer. _run_signal_probe (216-242) never touches _pending_signal. Deterministic trace: R1 runs inline holding _probe_lock; R2 queued during R1 gets the "выполнится автоматически" reply; when R1 finishes it drains R2 into a fire-and-forget asyncio task (209-210) and R1's handler returns. While that R2 task holds the lock, an R3 hits _probe_lock.locked()==True, sets …[обрезано]

### runtime/tick_io.py
- **Назначение:** Rotates hunt_scan tick JSONL into daily files with gzip archival + 14-day retention, and size-rotates append-only telemetry JSONL logs.
- **Методная опора:** no method basis (pure log-rotation/retention infra; no Prizrak/Owner-of-Shorts/Spekulyantka semantics; no signal or stat is derived here)
- **G-64** ✅ — **dry_run mutates state: the append branch writes to the daily file without a dry_run guard**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/tick_io.py:42-46` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 29 declares dry_run. Every other mutation is guarded: shutil.move (line 48 `if not dry_run`), the source truncate (line 52 `if not dry_run and ...`), and gzip+unlink (line 65 `if not dry_run`). But the `if daily.exists():` branch at lines 42-46 unconditionally does `for line in src: dst.write(line)` into daily.open('a'). No `if not dry_run` wraps it. So a dry_run call, whenever the day's daily file already exists, physically appends all of source's lines to the daily file. Because line 52's truncate IS dry-run-guarded, source is NOT emptied, so a subsequent real run re-appends the same lines -> duplicated ticks.
  - **Репро:** Given data/hunt_scan.jsonl >=1024 bytes and an existing data/hunt_scan-<today>.jsonl. Call rotate_hunt_ticks(dry_run=True): the daily file grows by source's line count and source is left intact; the next real rotate_hunt_ticks() double-appends the same lines.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Wrap the write loop in `if not dry_run:` (still increment stats['appended_lines'] so the dry-run report stays accurate), mirroring the move/truncate/prune guards.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None -- dry_run is never passed by either caller (_cycle_loop.py:234,1068 and :237,1071 call with no args) and no test exercises it; latent correctness bug only.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — Code at hunt_core/runtime/tick_io.py:42-46 matches the finding exactly. The `if daily.exists():` append branch opens source and daily in append mode and unconditionally writes every line (`for line in src: dst.write(line)`) with NO `if not dry_run` guard. Meanwhile every other side effect IS guarded: shutil.move at line 48 (`if not dry_run`), source truncate at line 52 (`if not dry_run and source == HUNT_SCAN_JSONL`), and gzip+unlink at lines 65-68 (`if not dry_run`). ### runtime/tick_state.py
- **Назначение:** Two-plane in-memory last-tick row cache (hunt scan plane vs deep query plane) with JSONL tail fallback, exposed via module-level singletons.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis — pure runtime storage/infra; not a signal feature.
- 🟡 *гипотеза* — **Pinned symbols are written to the hunt store every tick but resolve()/get() for pinned reads ONLY the deep store — freshest pinned tick is unreachable**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/tick_state.py:137 (resolve pinned branch) and 129-130 (get pinned branch); accurate as stated` · класс B / contract / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** cycle/_cycle_tick.py:497 does `hunt_scan_store().put_many(rows)`, and `rows` includes pinned symbols: the only pinned exclusion in that loop is the feature_lake gate at _cycle_tick.py:315 (`symbol not in PINNED_SYMBOLS`); every non-error row (pinned included) is appended at _cycle_tick.py:369 and gets row['plane']='hunt'. So the freshest per-scan-tick fusion row for a pinned symbol lands in the HUNT store. But LastTickStore.resolve() (tick_state.py:136-138) and .get() (tick_state.py:128-130) short-circuit for pinned to `self.deep.*` only, never consulting `self.hunt`. The deep store for pinned is refreshed only on-demand (analyst_assembly.py:309, query_service.py:384 bg refresh, signal_queue.py:259), not every tick. symbol_probe.py:138 uses `last_tick_store().resolve(sym)` on the /signal path and then age-gates it (`age <= STORE_STALE_S`); for a pinned symbol this reads the staler deep row (or ANALYST_TICKS_JSONL tail) while a fresher hunt row exists.
  - **Репро:** Call last_tick_store().put_hunt('BTCUSDT', fresh_row) (as put_many does for a pinned symbol) then last_tick_store().resolve('BTCUSDT') with the deep store empty/older: it returns the deep/jsonl row, never the fresh hunt row. Concrete: after a scan tick updates BTC in the hunt store but before any deep query, /signal BTC resolves the older deep-plane row.
  - **Мин. фикс:** If plane isolation for pinned is intended, stop writing pinned rows into the hunt store (skip pinned in the put_many at _cycle_tick.py:497); if freshness is intended, have resolve()/get() for pinned also consult self.hunt (e.g. return the age-freshest of deep vs hunt). Pick one so producer and reader agree.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** On /signal for a pinned major, the message can currently carry an older deep-plane price/levels snapshot (or trigger an avoidable live REST probe — the 418-ban path query_service warns about) instead of the just-computed scan-tick numbers.

## Чанк 3 — track

### track/_cooldowns.py
- **Назначение:** TG-delivery rate-limit / cooldown gates: post-stop reentry, global confirm-burst cap, per-symbol loss-streak, daily-cap, and chronic-repeat-loser blocks read off tracker closed_history + archived signal_history.jsonl.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis.
- **G-67** ✅ — **Confirmed manipulation signal records the global confirm-burst twice → burst cap of 2 trips after a single ping**
  - `Redundant call is manipulation_delivery.py:629; interacts with tracker.py:551 (unconditional record inside register_signal_open) and _cooldowns.py:63 (no-dedup append). All three cited locations are accurate.` · класс C / logic / **P1**
  - **Доказательство:** grep shows record_confirm_burst is invoked from exactly two sites: tracker.py:551 (inside register_signal_open) and manipulation_delivery.py:629. The main confirm lane (emitter.py:85) calls ONLY register_signal_open, so it records the burst once. The manipulation confirmed lane calls register_signal_open at manipulation_delivery.py:614 — which internally records the burst at tracker.py:551 with now=now_dt — and THEN calls record_confirm_burst again at line 629 with the same now_dt. record_confirm_burst (_cooldowns.py:63-78) appends now.isoformat() with no dedup, so confirm_burst_ts receives two identical timestamps for one signal. global_confirm_burst_cap_reached (_cooldowns.py:81-102) counts both (both >= cutoff) → count reaches GLOBAL_CONFIRM_BURST_MAX=2 after ONE confirmed manip signal. The manipulation_delivery.py:627 comment ('Track the burst window only AFTER a real send') shows the author did not know register_signal_open already records it.
  - **Репро:** tracker_state={'signals':{},'confirm_burst_ts':[]}; drive the manipulation confirmed path (micro_confirmed=True) once at time T for SYM-A. Inspect tracker_state['confirm_burst_ts'] → 2 identical ISO timestamps. Then global_confirm_burst_cap_reached(state, now=T)==True. A second manip confirm for SYM-B within 5 min is blocked at manipulation_delivery.py:537 though only one signal has actually shipped.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Delete the redundant record_confirm_burst(tracker_state, now=now_dt) call at manipulation_delivery.py:629; register_signal_open at line 614 already records the burst once (tracker.py:551), matching the main lane.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** Before: after one manipulation confirm, the next genuine manipulation setup on any symbol within a 5-min window is silently withheld from Telegram (cap hit at 1). After: up to 2 confirms per 5-min window ship as configured, so a second real setup still reaches subscribers.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — All three cited locations verified against the code:

1. `_cooldowns.py:63-78` — `record_confirm_burst` appends `now.isoformat()` to `confirm_burst_ts` with NO dedup. Confirmed exactly as claimed. `GLOBAL_CONFIRM_BURST_MAX = 2`, window = 5.0 min (`_cooldowns.py:13-14`).

2. `tracker.py:551` — the last statement of `register_signal_open` (function starts at tracker.py:446, verified via awk) is `record_confirm_burst(state, now=now)`, executed unconditionally on every open.

3. `manipulation_delivery.py:614` calls `register_signal_open(...)` (which internally records the burst once at 551), and t …[обрезано]
- **G-72** ✅ — **symbol_daily_tg_cap_reached sorts by closed_at but breaks the scan on opened_at → daily spam cap under-enforced for long-held trades**
  - `hunt_core/track/_cooldowns.py:194 (sort key=closed_at) vs 216/225 (break key=opened_at)` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** telegram_outcome_records sorts ascending by closed_at (_cooldowns.py:194: key = closed_at or opened_at). symbol_daily_tg_cap_reached iterates reversed(...) = descending by closed_at, but its cutoff test (line 216 raw=opened_at or closed_at; line 225 if opened < cutoff: break) uses OPENED time. A trade opened >24h ago but closed recently sorts LAST in ascending order → FIRST in the reversed scan → its opened_at < cutoff fires the break immediately, terminating the count before other trades that were opened within 24h but closed earlier (which sit later in the reversed order) are ever counted. Because break only truncates early, the error is always an UNDERCOUNT, so the per-symbol daily cap under-blocks (lets extra confirms through). The Prizrak/manipulation method holds positions long ('пересиживание'), so recently-closed-but-long-held trades are a realistic input.
  - **Репро:** state closed_history (all telegram_sent=True, SYM=X, dir=long): A opened now-25h closed now-1h; B opened now-2h closed now-2h; C opened now-3h closed now-3h. telegram_outcome_records sorts by closed_at → [C, B, A]; reversed → [A, B, C]. Loop hits A first: opened now-25h < cutoff(now-24h) → break, count=0. B and C (opened within 24h) never counted → symbol_daily_tg_cap_reached returns False though 2 same-day trades already exist; a 3rd confirm that should be capped is allowed.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Make the break key match the sort key: sort telegram_outcome_records by opened_at (or replace the early break in symbol_daily_tg_cap_reached with a plain continue so all in-window records are counted regardless of ordering).

### track/path_backfill.py
- **Назначение:** Backfills the D (forward-path) half of candidate_ledger entries: fetches raw 1m OHLCV for a candidate's [t0, t0+H_max] window and derives MFE/MAE/ret_at_offsets/first_passage_grid as an offline research cache.
- **Методная опора:** No direct channel-method basis. This is B4 research/backtest infrastructure (forward-path outcome ledger for precision@k / gate-blindness analysis), not a live-signal feature — sanity-check tier only.
- **G-86** ✅ — **path_backfill_loop is permanently inert: its only data source (decision rows) is never written by anyone**
  - `hunt_core/track/path_backfill.py:131 (run_backfill_pass -> load_pending_backfill); root cause hunt_core/track/candidate_ledger.py:44 (record_candidate_decision, zero callers). Location as claimed is correct.` · класс D / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** path_backfill_loop is unconditionally scheduled in non-once mode (hunt_core/runtime/cycle/_cycle_loop.py:445-449, logs 'path_backfill_scheduled'). run_backfill_pass calls load_pending_backfill (line 131), which returns ONLY rows with record_kind=='decision' (candidate_ledger.py:175). The sole writer of a record_kind=='decision' row is record_candidate_decision (candidate_ledger.py:101). grep across the entire repo (hunt_core, tests, scripts, research, *.toml) for 'record_candidate_decision' returns exactly ONE hit — its own definition in candidate_ledger.py — i.e. ZERO callers. (maybe_append_candidate_ledger in outcome_ledger.py:190 writes a DIFFERENT file/schema via append_ledger_event, not candidate_observations.jsonl.) Therefore candidate_observations.jsonl never receives a decision row, load_pending_backfill always returns [], run_backfill_pass returns 0 on every pass forever, and the 15-min loop does real work never. compute_derived_from_path / record_candidate_forward_path are correct code that can never be reached at runtime.
  - **Репро:** Start `python -m hunt_core watch` (non-once). Observe 'path_backfill_scheduled' then 'path_backfill_loop_start' in logs; candidate_observations.jsonl is never created (no decision rows produced anywhere in the code path) so run_backfill_pass returns 0 on every 15-min tick indefinitely. No 'path_backfill_pass done=' line ever appears.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either wire record_candidate_decision into the detector's per-candidate decision path (so decision rows actually get logged), or stop scheduling path_backfill_loop in _cycle_loop.py until the decision-logging half is wired. As-is the loop only burns a task slot and logs. (This may be intentional not-yet-wired B4 scaffolding — if so, gate the scheduling behind a flag rather than running an eternal no-op.)
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text — this is an offline research ledger with no delivery surface. Impact is silent: the forward-path outcome dataset the loop advertises to build is never populated.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — Could not refute; every claim reproduced via static analysis. (1) path_backfill.py:131 is `load_pending_backfill(now_ms=now_ms, max_rows=max_rows)` and run_backfill_pass returns 0 when it's empty (lines 132-133). (2) load_pending_backfill only ever surfaces rows with record_kind=="decision" (candidate_ledger.py:175 is the only branch feeding the `decisions` dict). - ❌ *REFUTED* — **first_passage_grid keys collapse favorable and adverse touches of the same |ATR| magnitude into one direction-less slot**
  - `hunt_core/track/path_backfill.py:81-90 and 109-114` · класс B / logic / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** first_touch[g] is a single slot per magnitude g. It is set by EITHER the adverse branch (line 82: adv_move <= -g) OR the favorable branch (line 89: fav_move >= g), whichever fires first, and the output key is only the magnitude: f"{g}atr" (line 110). Direction is not stored. Worked example, g=1.0, long: if low reaches -1.0 ATR at bar 5 and high reaches +1.0 ATR at bar 20 -> grid['1.0atr']=5min (an adverse/SL touch). If instead high hits +1.0 at bar 8 and low never reaches -1.0 -> grid['1.0atr']=8min (a favorable/TP touch). Both produce an identical-shaped '1.0atr' value with no field distinguishing a win-touch from a loss-touch. A consumer reading first_passage_grid alone cannot compute the win-rate of a +-1 ATR bracket. Mitigation: forward_ohlcv is retained and the module docstring states the derived block is a cache to be re-derived from the path, so this is lossy-by-design rather than data loss.
  - **Репро:** compute_derived_from_path(direction='long', entry=100, atr=1, decision_ts_ms=0, forward_ohlcv=[[0,100,100,100,100,1],[60000,100,100,98.9,99,1]]) -> first_passage_grid contains '1.0atr': 1.0 which is an ADVERSE touch, but is indistinguishable in shape from a favorable +1 ATR touch produced by a rising bar.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Split the grid into signed keys, e.g. emit both f"+{g}atr" (favorable, driven by fav_move>=g) and f"-{g}atr" (adverse, adv_move<=-g) from two separate first_touch maps, so downstream scoring can tell a TP-touch from an SL-touch without re-parsing forward_ohlcv.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No Telegram text change (offline cache). Downstream backtest/analysis code that trusts first_passage_grid without re-deriving from forward_ohlcv would mislabel loss-touches as wins for symmetric brackets.
  - **Вердикт:** REFUTED — The mechanical description is accurate: first_touch (line 64) is one slot per ATR magnitude g, written by the adverse branch (line 82, adv_move <= -g) or the favorable branch (line 89, fav_move >= g) — whichever fires first — and emitted under a direction-less key f"{g}atr" (line 110). The repro reproduces. However this is documented, intended behavior, not a defect: the module docstring (lines 1-13) and candidate_ledger.py:125-126 explicitly state the derived block is a denormalized cache that must NEVER be trusted alone, and that all TP/SL scoring is done offline against forward_ohlcv, which …[обрезано]

## Чанк 4 — data

### data/baseline_store.py
- **Назначение:** Persistent per-symbol rolling baselines with robust multi-TF z-scores for expansion-readiness scoring.
- **Методная опора:** No direct channel-method basis — internal quant scaffolding feeding the expansion_readiness accumulation/spring lane.
- **G-94** ✅ — **_append drops all funding rate samples <= 0, biasing the funding baseline; funding is legitimately negative**
  - `hunt_core/data/baseline_store.py:99 (guard) and :121 (funding fed through it); consumed at :151/:159` · класс C / calc / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** _append: `if value is None or value <= 0: return series`. The SAME guard feeds all five series including funding (line 121: `base.funding = _append(base.funding, fund)`, fund from row['funding_rate']). Perpetual funding on Binance USDⓈ-M is legitimately negative (shorts pay longs) and frequently exactly 0.0 — both are real measurements, not 'absent'. So base.funding can only ever accumulate strictly-positive funding samples. Any robust_z over that series is computed on a censored, upward-biased sample: negative-funding regimes are invisible and a real 0.0 funding print is discarded. The guard is correct for volume/quote_volume/oi/trade_count (0/negative = noise/absent) but wrong for a signed quantity. grep confirms base.funding is fed ONLY through this _append (baseline_store.py:121).
  - **Репро:** update_baseline_from_ticker('BTCUSDT', {'funding_rate': -0.0005}) repeated N times → load_baseline('BTCUSDT').funding == [] (every negative sample dropped). Feed alternating +0.0003/-0.0003 → only the positive halves survive, so the stored funding mean is strictly positive though true mean is ~0.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Split the guard: keep `value is None or value <= 0` for volume/quote_volume/oi/trade_count, but for funding filter only non-finite (already handled by _safe_float) — append signed values including 0.0. Simplest on existing data: add a `signed: bool=False` param to _append and pass signed=True at line 121.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any live Telegram signal today (funding_z is an unconsumed output — see companion finding). If funding_z were ever wired into expansion_readiness, negative-funding accumulation regimes would currently be silently excluded from the z, understating the anomaly.
  - **Вердикт:** CONFIRMED — The code at baseline_store.py:98-101 is exactly as described: `_append` returns the series unchanged when `value is None or value <= 0` (line 99), so it drops both negative and exactly-0.0 samples. Line 121 (`base.funding = _append(base.funding, fund)`) routes the signed funding rate (fund from row['funding_rate'], line 117) through this same unsigned guard, and grep confirms base.funding is fed ONLY through this one call site. Negative funding is legitimate market data on Binance USDⓈ-M (shorts pay longs) — the codebase itself treats it as meaningful: hunt_core/maps/liquidation.py:157 uses `- …[обрезано]
- **G-95** ✅ — **funding_z and volume_z_1h are orphan outputs — produced by baseline_zscores, read by no consumer**
  - `hunt_core/data/baseline_store.py:156,159 (funding_z produced at 159 via fund_z at 151; volume_z_1h at 156)` · класс B / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** grep for every consumer of baseline_zscores: the ONLY caller is hunt_core/scanner/detect/expansion_readiness.py:87, which reads exactly zs.get('volume_z_5m'), zs.get('volume_z'), zs.get('oi_z_5m'), zs.get('oi_z'), zs.get('trade_rate_z') (lines 107-109). The keys 'funding_z' (baseline_store.py:159) and 'volume_z_1h' (line 156) are never read anywhere — grep 'funding_z' across the repo hits only snapshot.py/collect.py's unrelated `funding_zscore_48h`/`get_cached_funding_rate_zscore`, and grep 'volume_z_1h' hits only baseline_store.py:156. Consequently the entire base.funding series (collected+persisted each cycle via batch_update_baselines→update_baseline_from_ticker) exists only to feed a dead key: fund_z = multi_tf_z(baseline.funding) at line 151 → funding_z, consumed by nobody.

### data/jsonl_io.py
- **Назначение:** Append-only JSONL writer with size-based log rotation and a best-effort "archive old rotated files" retention step for tick-buffer / audit / telemetry logs.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis — data-layer file plumbing, no channel-method signal logic.
- 🟡 *гипотеза* — **Archive step clobbers across rotation cycles: dest name has no generation/timestamp suffix, so os.rename silently overwrites — 'retention' archive keeps almost nothing**
  - `hunt_core/data/jsonl_io.py:22-23` · класс B / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** _archive_if_expired computes `dest = archive_dir / path.name` (line 22) and `shutil.move(str(path), str(dest))` (line 23). `path.name` for a rotated file is e.g. 'hunt_scan.jsonl.2' — a FIXED name per rotation-slot, carrying no cycle/timestamp discriminator. archive_dir is `path.parent / 'archive'` (line 20), i.e. same filesystem, so shutil.move dispatches to os.rename, which on POSIX overwrites an existing destination file silently. Rotation cycle N archives `.1/.2/.3` (when mtime>7d) into archive/foo.jsonl.1|.2|.3; cycle N+1 archives its own `.1/.2/.3` into the SAME three names, overwriting cycle N's copies. Net: the archive/ dir retains at most `keep` files total (one per slot, always the most-recently-archived), NOT a growing 7-day+ history. The line-9 comment ('Task 5: archive rotated files older than this') implies preservation/retention; the implementation preserves at most one generation. Reachability of `.1` being archived: `.1` mtime = last write to the live file before it filled to max_bytes; on a low-volume stream that fill can take >7d, so even `.1` is eligible and the clobber path is live, not just `.3`.
  - **Репро:** Set max_age_days=0 to force archiving. Create foo.jsonl.1 with content 'A', call _archive_if_expired(foo.jsonl.1) -> archive/foo.jsonl.1 == 'A'. Recreate foo.jsonl.1 with content 'B', call again -> archive/foo.jsonl.1 == 'B'; content 'A' is gone. Asserting two distinct archived generations survive fails.
  - **Мин. фикс:** In _archive_if_expired, disambiguate the destination on existing data instead of overwriting: e.g. `dest = archive_dir / f"{path.name}.{int(mtime)}"` (mtime is already computed at line 17), or skip the move when dest already exists. No new deps/data — uses the mtime already in scope.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text — this is offline log-retention plumbing; only historical tick/audit archive completeness is affected.
  - **Вердикт:** PLAUSIBLE — Code matches the finding exactly. Line 20-23: archive_dir = path.parent / "archive" (same filesystem), dest = archive_dir / path.name, shutil.move(str(path), str(dest)). Caller at lines 57-60 archives slot-named rotated files foo.jsonl.1/.2/.3 each rotation. path.name is a fixed per-slot name with no cycle/timestamp suffix.

I reproduced the clobber in Python: shutil.move of a same-basename file into an existing archive/foo.jsonl.1 overwrites via os.rename on POSIX; content 'A' is lost, only later 'B' survives, archive dir keeps exactly one file per slot. So the archive retains at most `keep`  …[обрезано]

### data/lake.py
- **Назначение:** Off-hot-path batch flush layer: buffers tick JSONL, tracker/cooldown state (with concurrent-write merge), map snapshots, and feature-parquet lake reads/writes.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis — pure infrastructure/persistence plumbing supporting the tracker and outcome-stats layers.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **closed_history merge dedups by full-record JSON identity, contradicting the producer's leg-key uniqueness → same trade leg can survive twice and double-count in the Telegram outcome digest**
  - `hunt_core/data/lake.py:82` · класс C / logic / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** Producer tracker.py:745-756 archives one record per open→close LEG and enforces uniqueness via outcome_archive_key = (symbol, direction, opened_at) (outcomes.py:95-104): before append it scans history and returns early if a rec with the same leg_key exists — closed_at/mfe/mae are deliberately NOT part of leg identity. But _merge_tracker_state (lake.py:82) dedups the disk+buffer union by `json.dumps(rec, sort_keys=True)` — the ENTIRE record. When the two unlocked loops the module's own docstring describes (per-tick + reconcile, each with its own load_tracker_state copy, no re-read) both close the same leg in the same beat, each snapshots a slightly different closed_at / mfe / mae / tp1_progress_pct, so record_A != record_B by full-json → BOTH are kept (line 83 never matches). Downstream telegram_outcome_records (_cooldowns.py:157-195) then dedups by (symbol,direction,opened_at,CLOSED_AT) — closed_at IS in its key — so the two records with divergent closed_at are NOT collapsed and the same closed trade is emitted twice in the outcomes/results digest and counted twice in any closed-leg stat.
  - **Репро:** Construct on_disk={'closed_history':[{'symbol':'BTC','direction':'long','opened_at':'2026-07-14T00:00:00Z','closed_at':'2026-07-14T01:00:00Z','telegram_sent':True,'mfe':1.0}]} and buffered={'closed_history':[{...same symbol/direction/opened_at...,'closed_at':'2026-07-14T01:00:05Z','telegram_sent':True,'mfe':1.2}]}; call _merge_tracker_state → merged['closed_history'] has length 2 for one leg; feed to _cooldowns.telegram_outcome_records → returns 2 records. Producer semantics (outcome_archive_key …[обрезано]
  - **Мин. фикс:** In the loop at lake.py:81-86 compute identity via outcome_archive_key(rec) (import from hunt_core.track.outcomes) when it returns non-None, falling back to the current json.dumps only when the leg key is None. That makes the merge's leg-uniqueness match the producer's.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** A single closed trade can appear twice in the periodic outcomes/results digest (two lines, two slightly different close prices/R for the same entry), inflating the reported win/loss count; after the fix each closed leg appears once.

### data/lake_warmup.py
- **Назначение:** Backfills the parquet feature lake for cold-start symbols from 15m OHLCV so freshly-promoted scanner candidates aren't NEUTRAL on the first tick.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis — infrastructure/warmup plumbing, not a channel method (Prizrak/Owner-of-Shorts/Spekulyantka).
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Dead int/float ts branch → warmup writes lake `ts` in a different format AND semantic than the live writer**
  - `hunt_core/data/lake_warmup.py:128-134` · класс C / contract / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** ts_col resolves to the first of ('close_time','open_time','ts','time') present in work_15m.columns. The klines frame from client.fetch_klines_cached is built by ccxt_ohlcv_to_frame (hunt_core/market/factory.py:442-447), which converts close_time/open_time/time to pl.Datetime('us','UTC') BEFORE _prepare_frame runs; _coerce_temporal_columns (prepare_frame.py:207-233) then skips them (already temporal). So `raw = work_15m.item(idx, ts_col)` at line 129 is ALWAYS a python datetime, and `isinstance(raw,(int,float))` at line 130 is ALWAYS False → the .isoformat() branch (lines 131-132) is unreachable dead code. Every warmup row therefore stores `ts_val = str(datetime)` = e.g. '2026-07-14 12:00:00+00:00' (space separator, bar-CLOSE time). The live writer stores a different value: _cycle_tick.py:333 enqueues `str(row.get('ts'))` where row['ts'] = now.isoformat() (_cycle_tick.py:251/75) = '2026-07-14T12:34:56.789+00:00' (T separator, wall-clock TICK time). The lake `ts` column thus holds two incompatible formats and two different semantics depending on which writer produced the row.
  - **Репро:** await backfill_cold_lake_symbol(client,'AAVEUSDT'); then pl.read_parquet(_parquet_path('AAVEUSDT','15m'))['ts'] → space-separated bar-close strings. Compare with a live-written row's ts (T-separated wall-clock). Marked hypothesis for signal impact because the only current consumers of query_features/read_features (lake_warmup.py:43 skip-check and _cycle_loop.py:751 cold-check) use .height row-counts and never parse ts, so no live signal is distorted today; the defect is a latent format/semantic  …[обрезано]
  - **Мин. фикс:** Replace lines 128-134 with a single format that matches the live convention, e.g. `ts_val = raw.isoformat() if hasattr(raw,'isoformat') else str(raw)`. This deletes the dead int/float guard and emits T-separated ISO strings identical in format to the live path (bar-close vs tick-time semantic difference remains but at least the string format is unified). No new deps/layers/data.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None. The lake ts is internal-only and never surfaced in Telegram signal text; this is lake hygiene, invisible to the owner.

### data/symbol_blacklist.py
- **Назначение:** Process-local TTL blacklist that suppresses re-fetching symbols that threw ccxt.BadSymbol (delisted/halted) for 1h.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis; this is data-plane resilience. Findings are tier-2 (internal contract consistency).
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Kline BadSymbol never reaches blacklist_symbol() — context is 'klines.<tf>' (no symbol), so the store's main producer is dead**
  - `hunt_core/data/collect.py:152-157 (extractor) + tick_assembly.py:371, collect.py:636/660/670 (kline contexts)` · класс C / contract / **P1**
  - **Доказательство:** symbol_blacklist.blacklist_symbol() has exactly one caller (collect.py:103), fed by _extract_symbol_from_context(context) (collect.py:148). That extractor's docstring claims context 'klines.BTCUSDT.1m', but every kline fetch actually emits context=f"klines.{name}" where name is a TIMEFRAME (tick_assembly.py:371 loops _base_tfs=('1m','5m','15m','1h','4h','1d','1w'); collect.py:636 is literal "klines.1m"; collect.py:660/670 same). grep 'context=f?"klines' returns ONLY these timeframe forms — no context ever contains the symbol. Recomputation of the extractor on the real string: extract('klines.15m') -> '15m'.replace('.',' ').split()=['15m'] -> '15M' ends with none of USDT/USD/BTC/ETH -> returns None (verified by executing the function). Per-tick kline fetches are THE primary BadSymbol source for a delisted/halted symbol, yet they extract nothing, so blacklist_symbol() is never called for them. Net: is_blacklisted() at _cycle_loop.py:759 removes almost nothing; the delisted symbol is re-fetched every tick, re-throwing BadSymbol indefinitely — defeating the module's entire purpose.
  - **Репро:** def _extract_symbol_from_context('klines.15m') returns None (assert). Add a delisted symbol to the universe: each tick logs safe_fetch_bad_symbol for klines.<tf>, is_blacklisted(sym) stays False forever, symbol never leaves the tick batch.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Carry the symbol in the kline context so it matches the extractor's documented format: at tick_assembly.py:371 and collect.py:660/670 use context=f"klines.{symbol}.{name}" (symbol is already in lambda scope). Then extract('klines.BTCUSDT.15m') -> 'BTCUSDT' (verified).
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No signal number changes (resilience path). Before: a delisted/halted symbol lingers in the universe and every tick spams BadSymbol on its klines, burning REST budget and producing degraded-data ticks; the blacklist filter is inert. After: the symbol is suppressed for 1h after the first failure and dropped from the tick batch, so it silently stops appearing instead of repeatedly failing.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Colon-format fetch contexts store phantom blacklist keys (e.g. 'FUNDING_RATE:BTCUSDT') that never match a universe symbol**
  - `hunt_core/data/collect.py:152 (_extract_symbol_from_context replace chain)` · класс C / contract / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** The extractor only splits on whitespace after .replace('klines.','').replace('.',' '); it never splits on ':'. Most per-symbol contexts use ':' (client.py:1041 funding_rate:{sym}, :794 open_interest:{sym}, :758 order_book:{sym}, market/spot.py:116 spot_ticker:{sym}). Executed: extract('funding_rate:BTCUSDT') -> 'FUNDING_RATE:BTCUSDT' (single token, endswith 'USDT' True). blacklist_symbol stores key 'FUNDING_RATE:BTCUSDT'.upper(); later is_blacklisted('BTCUSDT') (universe uses raw 'BTCUSDT', per universe.py:15 _CANONICAL_PINNED and s.upper() at _cycle_loop.py:645/716) looks up 'BTCUSDT' and misses -> a phantom entry that expires unused. Double-colon contexts extract nothing: extract('oi_change:BTCUSDT:5m') -> None, extract('basis:BTCUSDT:5m') -> None (verified).
  - **Репро:** assert _extract_symbol_from_context('funding_rate:BTCUSDT') == 'FUNDING_RATE:BTCUSDT'; blacklist_symbol(that); assert is_blacklisted('BTCUSDT') is False  # phantom, never consumed.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Split on ':' as well as '.': add .replace(':',' ') to the chain at collect.py:152. Then 'funding_rate:BTCUSDT' -> tokens include 'BTCUSDT', and 'oi_change:BTCUSDT:5m'/'basis:BTCUSDT:5m' also resolve.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No signal-text change. Before: funding/OI/order-book/spot BadSymbol failures either store an un-matchable key or nothing, so those paths also fail to blacklist the symbol. After: a BadSymbol on any of those fetches correctly suppresses the symbol, reducing repeated failed fetches on delisted assets.

## Чанк 5 — levels

### levels/levels.py
- **Назначение:** Structural entry-zone / SL / TP-ladder geometry for hunt watch shorts and longs, with adaptive volatility caps and a delivery-time re-anchor helper.
- **Методная опора:** SL/TP geometry port (Prizrak local-pivot SL + fib/liquidity TP ladder). Live pipeline uses only fib_retracement_levels and the min-SL-distance floors from this file; the structural builders and delivery-time reanchor are not wired.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **reanchor_setup_levels is the sole producer of levels_viable/levels_veto but has zero callers → the delivery-time levels veto gate is permanently inert**
  - `hunt_core/levels/levels.py:1458 (writes levels_viable/levels_veto at 1599-1600); consumed at hunt_core/runtime/tick_assembly.py:95,103, hunt_core/track/events.py:347, hunt_core/confluence/mtf.py:276-277` · класс C / contract / **P1**
  - **Доказательство:** grep 'reanchor_setup_levels' across the whole repo (*.py/*.toml) returns only the def at levels.py:1458 and one docstring/comment mention in mtf.py:221 — no call site anywhere (no getattr/importlib/__all__ re-export; levels/__init__.py says 'import directly'). This function is the ONLY writer of the keys 'levels_viable' (1599) and 'levels_veto' (1600): grep for those quoted keys shows every other hit is a reader (setup.get / dump.get / long_setup.get) or a contract.py schema field or a deliver/geometry.py label — no other producer. tick_assembly.py:95/103 does `if setup.get('levels_viable') is False or setup.get('levels_veto'): return False, ['veto_levels:...']` — a live gate that rejects a confirmed dump when geometry is non-viable. Because nothing ever calls reanchor_setup_levels, setup['levels_viable'] is always absent → `.get() is False` is never True and `.get('levels_veto')` is always falsy, so this gate (and the mtf.py `is not False` / events.py `if not ...` checks) can never fire.
  - **Репро:** Feed any confirmed short/dump setup dict (as built by the live scanner path) into runtime/tick_assembly.py's confirm-sticky gate. Because no upstream stage calls reanchor_setup_levels, the setup carries neither 'levels_viable' nor 'levels_veto'; line 95 and line 103 both evaluate False and the setup passes the geometry gate unconditionally, even when its entry/SL/TP would be non-viable (bad RR / stale late_chase) at delivery-time price.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Wire reanchor_setup_levels into the delivery/confirm path so it runs at delivery-time price and stamps levels_viable/levels_veto before tick_assembly's gate reads them; OR, if the live geometry is intentionally built elsewhere (track/_evaluate_levels.py, contract.py), delete the dead levels_viable/levels_veto consumer branches so the codebase does not advertise a safety gate that never fires. No new data needed.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** Today: a setup whose reanchored geometry would be vetoed is still delivered because the veto never populates. After wiring: such setups are suppressed (no message) instead of shipping a stale/late entry zone.

In playbook_archetype_key, `canon = canonical_archetype(name)`; the guard `if canon in {predump_short, prepump_long, ignition_long}: return canon` is false only when canon == 'none', and the else-branch then returns 'none' — identical to canon. So the function's output equals canonical_archetype(name) for every input; the branch never changes a value. Callers playbook_checks.py:51 and :66 could call canonical_archetype directly. (The Literal is also duplicated verbatim in manipulation_fusion.py:12 vs archetypes.py:6, but both are consistent.)

- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **falsy-zero in dead tf_label: rsi14==0.0 replaced by 50.0, defeating normalize_rsi14's oversold contract**
  - `hunt_core/toolkit/trend.py:161` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 161: `rsi = normalize_rsi14(_f(snap, "rsi14", 50.0))`. `_f` (line 24-28) does `float(snap.get(key, default) or default)`, so a genuine rsi14 of 0.0 evaluates `0.0 or 50.0` → 50.0. This directly contradicts normalize_rsi14's own docstring (line 32): 'Never scale valid oversold values like 1.0.' A true RSI floor (extreme oversold) would be reported as neutral 50. Only impact-limited because tf_label_from_snapshot itself is dead (see prior finding), so it never fires in production.
  - **Репро:** tf_label_from_snapshot({'adx14':10,'rsi14':0.0}, 'neutral') would return 'EMA переплетены' instead of 'Импульс нисходящий', because _f turns the 0.0 into 50.0 before the rsi<38 branch.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Fold into the dead-code removal above (delete the function). If instead the function is ever revived, read rsi with `_f(snap,'rsi14', default=50.0)` guarded by an explicit is-None check rather than `or default`, so a real 0.0 survives to normalize_rsi14.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No live signal change (function is dead).

### params/store.py
- **Назначение:** Unified hunt calibration store: universal delivery/geometry/liquidity gate defaults plus per-symbol overrides, merged from UNIVERSAL_DEFAULTS + config.defaults.toml forwarding + persisted hunt_calibration.json.
- **Методная опора:** No direct channel-method basis — config/contract infrastructure for delivery floors and geometry caps.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **[watch.prescan] TOML block is doc-only; prescan_thresholds() reads a section config.py never forwards, contradicting the TOML comment claiming it IS wired**
  - `hunt_core/params/store.py:437` · класс C / contract / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** prescan_thresholds() does `ps = universal_section("watch").get("prescan")`. universal_section("watch") = _deep_merge(UNIVERSAL_DEFAULTS.get("watch",{})={}, universal_section_from_defaults("watch"), overlay). Grep of hunt_core/domain/config.py::load_config_defaults_toml shows the forwarded sections are exactly {collect, delivery, fusion, intra_bar, scoring, tracker, confirm, deep, gates, hunter, levels, lifecycle} — there is NO `raw.get("watch")` handling (grep '"watch"|watch.prescan|prescan' hunt_core/domain/config.py returns nothing). So universal_section("watch") returns {}, .get("prescan") is None, and all four values fall back to literals. Yet config.defaults.toml:29-30 states: 'The NESTED [watch.prescan] below IS wired (params/store.py::prescan_thresholds via universal_section).' That claim is false. TOML keys debounce_s/merge_cap/cadence_s/max_change_pct_for_merge (config.defaults.toml:40-44) are read by nobody.
  - **Репро:** Edit config.defaults.toml [watch.prescan] debounce_s = 61, then call prescan_thresholds()['debounce_s'] → returns 90.0 (the literal fallback, clamped), not 61. The TOML edit is silently ignored.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either add a `raw.get('watch')` → out['watch'] = {'prescan': {...}} branch in load_config_defaults_toml so the section actually forwards, OR correct the config.defaults.toml comment (lines 29-30) to say [watch.prescan] is doc-only like the top-level [watch] keys. No behavior change needed today (TOML values already equal the fallbacks).
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None today — TOML values equal the fallbacks, so signal text is unchanged. The defect is that the owner cannot tune prescan debounce/merge cadence via the config file despite documentation saying he can.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **prescan_thresholds() emits 'cadence_s' which no consumer reads (orphan field)**
  - `hunt_core/params/store.py:443` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** prescan_thresholds() returns 'cadence_s': int(ps.get('cadence_s', 90)). Grep 'cadence_s' --include=*.py excluding params/store.py returns zero hits. The three real callers in runtime/cycle/_cycle_loop.py read only 'debounce_s', 'merge_cap', and 'max_change_pct_for_merge'. cadence_s is produced, read by nobody.
  - **Репро:** grep -rn cadence_s hunt_core --include='*.py' | grep -v params/store.py → empty.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Drop the 'cadence_s' key from the returned dict (and the corresponding TOML line if desired), or wire it at the prescan-loop call site if it was intended to drive cadence.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal — purely dead output.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **UNIVERSAL_DEFAULTS['hunter']['hot_range_pct'] = 8.0 is a stale dead key — hunter_thresholds() reads 'range_hot_pct', not 'hot_range_pct'**
  - `hunt_core/params/store.py:80` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** In the 'hunter' section base default (store.py:79-82) the key is 'hot_range_pct': 8.0, but hunter_thresholds() (store.py:420) reads sc.get('range_hot_pct', 8.0). config.defaults.toml [hunter] correctly uses range_hot_pct (line 15) and config.py forwards the whole [hunter] block under 'hunter'. Grep for any read of the hunter section's hot_range_pct: the only hot_range_pct consumers are levels.py:100 (reads from the 'levels' section caps / per-symbol, not 'hunter') and config.py:347 (forwards levels.hot_range_pct). Nothing reads hunter→hot_range_pct, so store.py:80 is a leftover from the old name and never influences anything.
  - **Репро:** grep the codebase: the hunter section key 'hot_range_pct' is written only at store.py:80 and never read; hunter_thresholds keys on 'range_hot_pct' instead.

  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change — the key never fed a threshold; removal only clears misleading dead config.


## Чанк 7 — domain+signals+diagnostics

### domain/config.py
- **Назначение:** Pydantic HuntSettings config models plus load_settings/load_config_defaults_toml, which parse config.toml [bot] and forward config.defaults.toml threshold blocks into params.store.universal_section().
- **Методная опора:** no method basis — pure config plumbing; forwarded blocks are calibration knobs, so TRUTH priority 2 (internal code consistency) governs.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **[fusion] and [intra_bar] TOML blocks forwarded to a dead end — real tuned values silently ignored, and [fusion]'s wiring comment is false**
  - `hunt_core/domain/config.py:371` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** config.py:371 `for section in ("collect", "scoring", "tracker", "delivery", "intra_bar", "fusion")` copies each block from config.defaults.toml into the universal-section store. Both [intra_bar] (config.defaults.toml:207) and [fusion] (config.defaults.toml:225) hold real values (q_gate=0.92, min_active_factors=2, fusion_score_scale=25.0; momentum_window=10, dom_imbalance_min=0.15, ...). But the only reader of a stored section is params/store.py::universal_section(section); grep of every `universal_section("...")` call across hunt_core lists collect/scoring/tracker/delivery but NEVER "fusion" or "intra_bar". The one dynamic reader (store.py:246 resolve_float) has zero external callers. Keys q_gate/min_active_factors/fusion_score_scale/q_phase and momentum_window/dom_imbalance_min/burst_min/sequence_window_seconds appear in NO consumer (grep -rln across repo → only store.py's UNIVERSAL_DEFAULTS + this forwarder). The [fusion] block header in config.defaults.toml asserts `These values are now actually read by fusion_params() via load_config_defaults_toml().` — `grep -rIn fusion_params --include=*.py .` returns nothing: fusion_params() does not exist anywhere in the repo.
  - **Репро:** In a REPL: `from hunt_core.params.store import universal_section; universal_section('fusion')` returns only store.py's hardcoded UNIVERSAL_DEFAULTS['fusion'] merged with an empty overlay — edit q_gate=0.92→0.50 in config.defaults.toml and the returned value is unchanged because nothing calls universal_section('fusion'). No test/import references fusion_params.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Drop "intra_bar" and "fusion" from the tuple at config.py:371 and delete the two orphan blocks (or the false comment) from config.defaults.toml; if the fusion engine is meant to read them, wire a real fusion_params() that calls universal_section('fusion'). No new data/deps.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No signal-text change. Editing the [fusion]/[intra_bar] blocks in config.defaults.toml is a silent no-op today; removing them (or the lying comment) stops the owner from believing those knobs are live.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **config.py forwards [lifecycle].squeeze, [collect], [scoring], [delivery], and [confirm] top-level to reader functions that have zero call-sites — doc-only config**
  - `hunt_core/domain/config.py:354` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** config.py:354-369 reads raw['lifecycle']['squeeze'] and re-emits under renamed keys (bb_width_pctile_max→squeeze_bb_width_pctile_max, taker_buy_min, cascade_wick_ratio_min, ...). Two-fold dead: (a) config.defaults.toml has NO [lifecycle] section (grep `^\[lifecycle` → none), so raw.get('lifecycle') is absent, isinstance(...,dict) is False, lifecycle_sq=None, block never built; (b) the only consumer path, params/store.py::lifecycle_thresholds() (universal_section('lifecycle')), has 0 external call-sites (grep -rIn '\blifecycle_thresholds\b' across repo incl tests/scripts, minus store.py/config.py = 0). The same deadness holds for the sections forwarded at config.py:371/395/402/476: collect_thresholds, scoring_thresholds, delivery_thresholds all have 0 external refs, and the top-level [confirm] path (config.py:314-325 → confirm_thresholds/entry_confirm_tf/dump_fast_confirm_enabled) also has 0 external refs. NOTE the one LIVE confirm path: [confirm.short] (config.py:327-337) feeds out['gates'], and effective_hunt_params()→gates IS consumed (track/events.py, runtime/symbol_probe.py) — so confirm.short must stay.
  - **Репро:** grep -rIn '\b(lifecycle_thresholds|collect_thresholds|scoring_thresholds|delivery_thresholds|confirm_thresholds|entry_confirm_tf|dump_fast_confirm_enabled)\b' --include='*.py' . | grep -v params/store.py | grep -v domain/config.py → 0 hits for every one. Editing [scoring] or [delivery] in config.defaults.toml therefore changes no runtime value.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Remove the lifecycle-squeeze forwarder (config.py:354-369) and drop collect/scoring/delivery + the top-level confirm-tf forwarding, keeping only sections with live readers (hunter, tracker, levels, gates via confirm.short, deep.prizrak). Prune the matching dead reader functions in store.py separately. Keep confirm.short.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No signal-text change — these blocks already have no runtime effect. Fix only stops silent no-op edits to config.defaults.toml from misleading the owner.

### domain/signal_horizon.py
- **Назначение:** Signal-horizon taxonomy (SCALP/INTRADAY/SWING/POSITION) mapping to TTL and cooldown minutes; derives a horizon from setup timeframes.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis. TTL/cooldown-by-horizon is an engineering construct; none of Prizrak / Owner-of-Shorts / Spekulyantka defines a scalp/swing TTL taxonomy. The channel methods use multi-day forward horizons and пересиживание, not fixed 120/3 …[обрезано]
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Entire module is a dead consumer chain — derive_signal_horizon and ttl_minutes_for_horizon have zero importers; cooldown_minutes_for_horizon is reachable only through production_cooldown_ok, which is never called anywhere**
  - `hunt_core/domain/signal_horizon.py:30-62` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**

Grepping `production_cooldown_ok` across the entire repo (*.py, *.md, *.toml) returns ONLY its own definition at delivery_state.py:39 — zero call sites, and it is not exported from hunt_core/deliver/__init__.py. Therefore: derive_signal_horizon → 0 importers; ttl_minutes_for_horizon → 0 importers; cooldown_minutes_for_horizon → 1 importer that is itself dead; SignalHorizon enum → referenced only inside this dead file. The whole module executes for nobody.
  - **Репро:** From repo root: `grep -rn 'production_cooldown_ok\|derive_signal_horizon\|ttl_minutes_for_horizon' --include='*.py' .` — every hit is either the definition site or the never-called production_cooldown_ok. No live call path reaches any function in this file.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Delete hunt_core/domain/signal_horizon.py and the dead production_cooldown_ok/cooldown import in delivery_state.py (same sweep that removed the G-25 modules); or, if TTL/cooldown-by-horizon is genuinely intended, wire production_cooldown_ok into the deliver cross-channel cooldown path. No signal logic depends on it either way.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None. The module never runs, so no Telegram signal text, TTL, or cooldown is currently affected; removal changes nothing users see.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Phantom fallback keys trigger_tf and pattern_tf are read but never produced anywhere in the repo**
  - `hunt_core/domain/signal_horizon.py:36-37` · класс C / contract / **P2**

The real setup dict producer (hunt_core/levels/levels.py:1168-1171, 1362-1365) writes only `source_tf` and `target_tf`, which are the primary keys read on lines 36-37, so the fallbacks are permanently dead branches.
  - **Репро:** `grep -rn 'trigger_tf\|pattern_tf' --include='*.py' --include='*.toml' --include='*.json' . | grep -v signal_horizon.py` returns empty.
  - **Мин. фикс:** If the module is kept, drop the `or setup.get('trigger_tf')` and `or setup.get('pattern_tf')` fallbacks since source_tf/target_tf are always the produced keys; otherwise this is subsumed by deleting the module.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None — these fallbacks never fire (they sit inside the already-dead derive_signal_horizon).

### domain/snapshot.py
- **Назначение:** Wraps each populated market-derivative field with {value, source, age_s} provenance and serializes it into a per-tick `snapshot` block.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis. Pure engineering/observability plumbing (Phase 2 / #45 provenance stamping); the Prizrak/Owner/Spekulyantka methods say nothing about per-field provenance wrappers.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **MarketSnapshot output is an orphan: the `snapshot` provenance block is written twice per tick and read by nobody**
  - `hunt_core/domain/snapshot.py:28 (from_market) → consumed at hunt_core/runtime/tick_assembly.py:801 and 874` · класс B / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** `MarketSnapshot.from_market(market).to_dict()` is the sole product of this module. It is written into the tick row twice: (a) tick_assembly.py:801 `market["_snapshot"] = _market_snapshot.to_dict()` — and since tick_assembly.py:857 embeds `"market": market`, this nests it under `result["market"]["_snapshot"]`; (b) tick_assembly.py:874 `"snapshot": _market_snapshot.to_dict()` — a second, byte-identical copy under `result["snapshot"]`. Grep for every reader across the whole repo returns nothing: `grep -rn '"_snapshot"|\["snapshot"\]|get("snapshot")' --include=*.py .` finds only the two write sites plus unrelated `.snapshot()` method calls and `snapshot_*` symbols; no code path reads `row["snapshot"]`, `market["_snapshot"]`, or `result["snapshot"]`. So the module runs on every symbol every tick, allocates a SnapshotField per populated field, and its result is either discarded or (at most) dead weight in serialized tick-audit JSONL. The write at :801 is additionally redundant with the :874 copy.
  - **Репро:** From repo root: `grep -rn '\["snapshot"\]\|get("snapshot")\|"_snapshot"' --include="*.py" . | grep -v tick_assembly.py` returns zero consumer sites, while tick_assembly.py:801 and :874 both write the block — proving produced-but-never-read.
  - **Мин. фикс:** On existing data only: drop the redundant `market["_snapshot"] = ...` at tick_assembly.py:801 (already carried by `result["market"]` and duplicated by `result["snapshot"]`). If the `snapshot` block is confirmed to serve no offline/audit purpose either, remove the `MarketSnapshot.from_market` call and this module entirely. No behavior depends on it. Do NOT add a consumer — none is required by any method.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text. The `snapshot` provenance block never reaches delivery; removing it is invisible to the owner and only reduces per-tick allocation and JSONL row size.

### domain/structure_state.py
- **Назначение:** Builds a typed StructureState snapshot (HTF trend, BOS/CHoCH, VA levels, bias, liquidity pool) from a tick row's structure/regime/lifecycle sub-dicts and stamps it onto result["structure_state"].
- **Методная опора:** Implements the Prizrak structure-first spine (H8): HTF trend + BOS/CHoCH event + POC/VAH/VAL + structure bias as a snapshot for the decision/query planes. No class-A method quote required; findings are internal contract contradictions.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **htf_trend_1h / htf_trend_4h read phantom keys — always collapse to "ranging"**
  - `hunt_core/domain/structure_state.py:53-54` · класс C / logic / **P1**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 53: htf_1h = regime.get("regime_1h_confirmed") or struct.get("structure_1h") or "ranging". Line 54: htf_4h = regime.get("regime_4h_confirmed") or struct.get("regime_4h_confirmed") or "ranging". The regime sub-dict is built by regime_snapshot() (features/snapshot.py:893-894) which stores the confirmed trends under keys 'regime_4h' and 'regime_1h' — NOT 'regime_1h_confirmed'/'regime_4h_confirmed'. grep 'regime_1h_confirmed|regime_4h_confirmed' over snapshot.py shows they appear only as prepared ATTRIBUTES on the RHS, never as dict keys. So regime.get('regime_1h_confirmed') and regime.get('regime_4h_confirmed') are always None. The struct fallbacks also miss: struct = assess_market_structure(...) (features/structure.py:461-480) emits key 'htf_trend', and has NO 'structure_1h' or 'regime_4h_confirmed' key (grep of struct-producing paths returns nothing; 'structure_1h' exists only inside the regime dict). Both OR chains therefore fall through to the "ranging" literal on every tick, for every symbol, regardless of actual 1h/4h regime.
  - **Репро:** Assemble a row where regime={'regime_1h':'uptrend_confirmed','regime_4h':'uptrend_confirmed', ...} (the real snapshot shape) and structure={'htf_trend':'uptrend', ...}. structure_state_from_row(row).htf_trend_1h == 'ranging' and .htf_trend_4h == 'ranging' despite a confirmed uptrend. Correct keys would yield 'uptrend_confirmed'.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Read the real keys: regime.get('regime_1h') for htf_1h and regime.get('regime_4h') for htf_4h; drop the dead struct fallbacks or point them at struct.get('htf_trend').
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No visible change today (see the orphan-output finding — nothing reads structure_state). Latent: the moment structure_state is wired into the decision/query plane as its docstring intends, every snapshot would silently report HTF trend = ranging, suppressing structure bias context.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **liquidity_pool reads phantom key 'liquidity_pool'/'pool' — producer emits 'liquidity_pools' (a nested dict)**
  - `hunt_core/domain/structure_state.py:84` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 84: pool = str(struct.get("liquidity_pool") or struct.get("pool") or ""). assess_market_structure (features/structure.py:466) emits the key 'liquidity_pools' (plural, value is the dict from _liquidity_pools()). There is no scalar 'liquidity_pool' or 'pool' key in the structure dict. So pool is always "", StructureState.liquidity_pool is always empty, and the reasons.append(f"pool={pool}") branch (line 88-89) is unreachable.
  - **Репро:** structure_state_from_row(row).liquidity_pool == "" for any row, even when structure['liquidity_pools'] is populated.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either drop the dead pool branch, or derive a scalar label from struct['liquidity_pools'] (e.g. its 'nearest_above'/'nearest_below' or a side tag).
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None today (output orphan). Removes a permanently-empty field / dead reason line so a future wiring doesn't silently omit pool context.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **level_kind reads phantom keys 'level_kind'/'setup_type' — neither exists in the structure dict**
  - `hunt_core/domain/structure_state.py:76` · класс C / logic / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 76: level_kind = str(struct.get("level_kind") or struct.get("setup_type") or ""). The structure dict from assess_market_structure (features/structure.py:461-480) contains none of: 'level_kind', 'setup_type'. grep shows 'setup_type' is produced only in track/events.py:94 on a separate 'setup' dict, never on the structure sub-dict. So level_kind is always "", and the guarded reason at line 90-91 (`if at_level and level_kind: reasons.append(f"at_{level_kind}")`) never fires.
  - **Репро:** structure_state_from_row(row).level_kind == "" for any row; the at_<kind> reason is never appended even when at_level is True.

- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **structure_state output is orphaned — computed every tick, read by no consumer**
  - `hunt_core/runtime/tick_assembly.py:1108` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** tick_assembly.py:1108 writes result["structure_state"] = structure_state_from_row(result).to_dict() on every tick. grep of the whole repo (*.py/*.toml/*.md/*.json) for 'structure_state' returns only the producer (domain/structure_state.py) and this single write site; grep for the output field names 'htf_trend_1h', 'htf_trend_4h', 'bos_choch_event' returns zero consumers. No decision-plane, delivery, or query-plane code reads it. The docstring claims it feeds 'decision + query planes' but nothing consumes it.

### signals/lifecycle.py
- **Назначение:** Signal lifecycle spine: computes stable setup_id, drives forming→signal→activated state transitions, and persists a per-setup_id cooldown/last-state store so Prizrak/Scanner rows emit only on real state advance.
- **Методная опора:** No direct channel-method basis — internal emission/dedup infrastructure (anti-spam plumbing around the Prizrak orchestrator's action/activation output). Method truth is upstream in the orchestrator that sets action/activation.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **setup_cooldown branch is unreachable — the SIG-1 'fix' comment overstates it; the 4h cooldown never fires**
  - `hunt_core/signals/lifecycle.py:200-201` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** The guard is `if event == "signal" and not store._cooldown_ok(setup_id)`. `event` is set to "signal" ONLY in the elif/else branches (lines 182-188), and only when `prev_state not in {"signal","activated","tracking"}`. `prev_state = store.last_state(setup_id)` reads the persisted entry's `state`. record_emit (line 131-138) always writes `state = signal.state`, and both record_emit callers (lifecycle.py:240, runtime/emitter.py:47) pass a Signal whose `state` was set by this same function to now_state ∈ {"signal","activated"} — never "forming"/"tracking". Grep confirms entries are NEVER deleted/pruned/expired (only .get/assignment on self.entries in the whole file). Therefore, once a setup_id has emitted once, prev_state is permanently in {signal,activated}, so every later tick returns at line 190-191 ("no_state_advance") BEFORE reaching line 200. The ONLY tick where event=="signal" is the first emission for a setup_id, where the entry is absent → _cooldown_ok returns True (line 117-118) → `not True` = False. Hence line 201 (`suppress_reason="setup_cooldown"`) can never execute. The oscillation scenario the comment describes ('oscillated out of and back into near-entry within 4h is su …[обрезано]
  - **Репро:** Unit test: build a row with prizrak_summary={action:'long', activation:'near_entry', entry_lo/hi/catalyst set}. Call process_lifecycle_tick(row, store=S, commit=True) → returns event='signal'. Call it again 1 minute later with the same row → asserts event=='none' and suppress_reason=='no_state_advance' (NOT 'setup_cooldown'). No sequence of inputs yields suppress_reason=='setup_cooldown'; assert it is unreachable.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either delete the dead branch (lines 193-201) since anti-spam is already fully provided by the 'no_state_advance' early-return, or — if a real 4h re-arm cooldown is wanted — evaluate _cooldown_ok independently of the event-advance gate (e.g. check it before the prev_state exclusion so a genuine re-form after 4h can re-emit). No new data needed.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to the Telegram signal text today: signals are already de-duplicated by the state-advance gate, so removing the dead branch is behavior-neutral. It only removes a misleading 'setup_cooldown' suppression reason that never appears in logs.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Redundant elif branch reads activation values (near_catalyst/at_catalyst) that are never present in prizrak_summary['activation']; elif and else are behavior-identical**
  - `hunt_core/signals/lifecycle.py:181-188` · класс C / contract / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** The elif at line 181 matches {"near_entry","near_catalyst","at_catalyst"} and the else at 185 both set now_state="signal" and use the identical event predicate `if prev_state not in {"signal","activated","tracking"}` — so the elif is a behavior-neutral distinction. Grep of all writers of summary['activation'] shows only orchestrator.py (579='idle', 1079='in_entry_zone', 1179='in_entry_zone'|'near_entry', 1298/1418='approaching'). assess_activation() (engines/activation.py) can produce 'near_catalyst'/'at_catalyst' but returns them in a separate dict stored into a queue-item at signal_queue.py:238, never into prizrak_summary['activation']. Therefore 'near_catalyst' and 'at_catalyst' are phantom values here — this branch can never match them. Separately, "tracking" in the exclusion sets (lines 183,187) is also never persisted: no record_emit caller passes a Signal with state=='tracking' (now_state is only ever 'signal'/'activated').
  - **Репро:** is_hypothesis: enumerate the 4 possible values orchestrator writes to summary['activation'] ('idle','in_entry_zone','near_entry','approaching') plus ''/None. 'in_entry_zone'→if-branch; every other value → else-branch produces the same now_state/event as the elif would. No input drives the elif's 'near_catalyst'/'at_catalyst' arms. Assert the elif is dead relative to the else.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Collapse the elif into the else (they are identical), OR — if the intent is that lifecycle should consume assess_activation's richer state — have the orchestrator write assess_activation's state into summary['activation'] so 'near_catalyst'/'at_catalyst' actually flow. Also drop 'tracking' from the exclusion sets since this store never persists it. Pure cleanup, no new data.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None. All non-'in_entry_zone' activations already map to a 'signal' event, so the emitted Telegram text is unchanged; this is dead-distinction cleanup only.

### signals/price_sanity.py
- **Назначение:** Suppression gate: withholds a long/short lifecycle signal when the live price deviates >25% from the mean of a set of reference price levels (market/structure/session anchors).
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis. Internal safety gate (docstring cites "plan §5.13"). Wired into process_lifecycle_tick (lifecycle.py:164) before a long/short setup can emit.

A definitive grep `grep -rn '["mark_price"] =|"mark_price":' hunt_core` finds mark_price ONLY in low-level premium/cross fetch dicts (market/client.py:1118-1119, market/cross.py:226) which snapshot.py:717-718 reads and re-maps into prepared.mark_price -> market['mark']; none land in row['market']. `grep -rn 'last_close_1h' hunt_core` returns ONLY price_sanity.py:22 -- zero producers. map_vp_poc IS valid (maps/engine.py:434 derive_map_features -> apply_map_bundle_to_row market.update(features)). Net: 3 of 4 market refs are dead; only map_vp_poc contributes. The mark/index quotes -- the truest current-price anchors the gate is meant to compare against -- are silently dropped.
  - **Репро:** Build a row as tick_assembly produces (row['market'] = {'mark': 50000.0, 'index': 50000.0, 'map_vp_poc': 49900.0}, no 'mark_price'/'index_price'/'last_close_1h' keys). Call price_sanity_check(row): the market loop appends only map_vp_poc; 'mark'/'index' are ignored. Setting market['mark']=1e9 does NOT change refs -- proving the anchor is never read.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Rename the market keys read to the real producer names: ('mark','index','map_vp_poc'); drop 'last_close_1h' (no producer). No new data.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** This is a suppression gate, so the effect is on WHICH signals get withheld. Today the reference mean is built from structural support/resistance/swings + VP POC only (levels that legitimately sit far from price), so a stale or wildly-off live quote can pass the 25% gate and a garbage signal reaches Telegram. After the fix the gate compares against the real mark/index (~ current price), so an impla …[обрезано]

  - `hunt_core/signals/price_sanity.py:44` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**

The row actually carries a 'session' key (tick_assembly.py:860 "session": session) built by session_stats() (features/snapshot.py:145-159), whose keys are high_24h/low_24h/range_pct_24h/pos_in_range/bars_1m_used -- none of price_high/price_low/last_price. - ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **prescan-ready audit reads readiness_direction and cross_venues off _DebouncedSymbol, which (slots) never carries them → always "" and 0**
