The real values DO exist upstream (PrescanHit carries readiness_direction/cross_venues, and _cycle_loop.py:606-608 stores them into prescan_outlier_by_sym) but PrescanDebounceQueue.offer (prescan.py:445-462) drops them when building _DebouncedSymbol.
  - **Репро:** Same run; every prescan_ready row has "readiness_direction":"" and "cross_venues":0 even for symbols whose PrescanHit had readiness_direction='long' / cross_venues=3. Assert a non-empty readiness_direction — fails.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Add readiness_direction and cross_venues fields to _DebouncedSymbol and copy them in PrescanDebounceQueue.offer (both the new-item and update branches), mirroring how oi_divergence is already carried; or drop the two always-constant columns from the audit record.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to Telegram signal text. Audit JSONL loses the readiness bias and multi-venue confirmation that explains why a symbol entered the universe — both fields are constant.

### diagnostics/universe_health.py
- **Назначение:** Pure per-tick aggregator that turns a silent universe-wide data-plane blackout into a loud degraded/critical operator signal + self-restart predicate.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis — this is operator/ops resilience infra (2026-07-11 proxy-death and 2026-07-13 stalled-mux incidents), pure internal-consistency territory.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **rest_error rows (timeout / network-exception blackout) are classified HEALTHY — the blackout detector misses the exact stall it was built for**
  - `hunt_core/diagnostics/universe_health.py:65-68 (regex def :28); producers hunt_core/runtime/cycle/_cycle_tick.py:250-256,257-265,74-80` · класс C / logic / **P0**

Verified none match the regex: re.search on 'symbol_tick_timeout'→False, "TimeoutError()"→False, "ClientConnectorError('proxy')"→False, "HuntDataError('boom')"→False, 'ConnectionResetError(54)'→False (only 'klines.4h.stale...'→True). classify_row_health therefore returns None for every rest_error row → it lands in `total` (denominator) but never in `kinds`/`failures` → failure_frac undercounts. A universe-wide stall/timeout blackout (the 2026-07-13 stalled-15m-WS-mux incident cited in should_self_restart_on_blackout's own docstring, which manifests as symbol_tick_timeout when snapshot_symbol hits SYMBOL_TICK_TIMEOUT_S) …[обрезано]

  - **Мин. фикс:** In classify_row_health, before the _DATA_ERROR_RE check, add: if row.get('tick_path')=='rest_error' (or: an `error` is truthy but unmatched) return a stable kind such as 'rest_error' (or _violation_kind(err)). Uses only fields already on the row (tick_path + error) — no new data. Add a test with a symbol_tick_timeout row asserting degraded/critical.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** Before: during a stall/timeout blackout the operator gets NO '🚨 Data blackout' Telegram message and the bot never self-restarts — it sits blind exactly as in the incident the module exists to prevent (failure_pct reads 0% while the whole universe is dead). After: timeout/network-error rows count as failures, failure_pct reflects the real blackout, the alert fires with the correct dominant_kind and …[обрезано]


## Чанк 8 — root

### __main__.py
- **Назначение:** Package CLI entry-point: `python -m hunt_core watch [flags]` parses four flags and forwards them to hunt_core._cli.main.
- **Методная опора:** no method basis
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **--interval forwarding guarded by a duplicated magic constant 30; explicit `--interval 30` is silently dropped**
  - `hunt_core/__main__.py:37` · класс C / contract / **P2** · (auditor: гипотеза)
  - **Доказательство:** __main__.py:27 `watch_p.add_argument("--interval", type=int, default=30)`; __main__.py:37-38 `if args.interval != 30: watch_argv.extend(["--interval", str(args.interval)])`; _cli.py:81 `watch_parser.add_argument("--interval", type=int, default=30)`. The value 30 is hardcoded in three places. The `!= 30` guard means an explicit `--interval 30` is never forwarded into sys.argv (__main__.py:16) — it only produces the correct behaviour because _cli.py's own default is also 30. If _cli.py's default is ever changed, `python -m hunt_core watch --interval 30` would silently run at the new default, not 30.
  - **Репро:** Change _cli.py:81 default to e.g. 60. Run `python -m hunt_core watch --interval 30`. Observed loop interval is 60s (default), not the requested 30s, because __main__.py:37 skips forwarding when args.interval==30.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Forward the flag unconditionally: replace the `if args.interval != 30:` guard with an always-append `watch_argv.extend(["--interval", str(args.interval)])` (the downstream parser already defaults it, so no double-default risk), or drop __main__.py's own `--interval` arg and let it pass through via `rest`.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to Telegram signal text today (both defaults are 30). Prevents a future silent scan-cadence mismatch if the downstream default is edited.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Unreachable fallthrough: print_help()/return 2 can never execute**
  - `hunt_core/__main__.py:45` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** __main__.py:23 `sub = parser.add_subparsers(dest="command", required=True)` — required=True makes argparse exit with SystemExit(2) before returning if no command is given. `watch` (line 25) is the only registered subparser, so when parse_known_args succeeds `args.command` is always "watch", making the `if args.command == "watch":` at line 33 always true and the trailing `parser.print_help(); return 2` (lines 45-46) unreachable.
  - **Репро:** No input reaches lines 45-46: omitting the command triggers argparse's own SystemExit(2) at parse_known_args (line 31); supplying `watch` satisfies the line-33 branch and returns at line 43.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Delete lines 45-46 (dead), or drop `required=True` if a help-on-no-command UX is actually intended (then the fallthrough becomes live).
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None — dead code, no runtime effect on signals or delivery.

### _cli.py
- **Назначение:** Thin argparse app-shell: parses `watch` args, installs SIGINT/SIGTERM stop handlers, takes a single-instance pid lock, and runs the async signal-watch loop.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis — pure runtime plumbing (process lifecycle, CLI arg parsing). Not an implementation of any channel-method feature.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Inert shebang: `#!/usr/bin/env python3` on line 3 after `from __future__ import annotations`, never honored**
  - `hunt_core/_cli.py:3` · класс D / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 1 is `from __future__ import annotations`; line 3 is `#!/usr/bin/env python3`. A shebang is only interpreted by the OS exec loader when it is the FIRST two bytes of the file (line 1, col 1). Here it sits on line 3, after a real statement, so Python treats it as an ordinary comment and the OS never sees it as an interpreter directive. The module is only ever launched via `python -m hunt_core` (see hunt_core/__main__.py `_cmd_watch` → `from hunt_core._cli import main`) — never executed directly — so the line is pure dead cosmetics. Confirmed by reading lines 1-4; no `chmod`/direct-exec path exists (grep of pyproject/scripts shows entry via module, not file).
  - **Репро:** Not runtime-observable. Static: `chmod +x hunt_core/_cli.py && ./hunt_core/_cli.py` would exec under the shell (not python3) because no valid line-1 shebang exists, producing a syntax error instead of running the CLI — demonstrating the directive is non-functional where placed.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Delete line 3 (the file is launched via `python -m`, so no shebang is needed). If a shebang is genuinely wanted, it must be the literal first line, before `from __future__ import annotations`.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text; this line never executes and touches no signal, stat, or output path.

### bootstrap.py
- **Назначение:** Startup shim: extend sys.path, set POLARS_STREAMING, patch aiohttp DNS resolver, init opt-in telemetry, and fail-fast if the Polars TA feature stack is missing.
- **Методная опора:** no method basis (infrastructure bootstrap, not a channel-method feature)
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Stale `pip install -e hunt/` remediation message and docstring point to a directory that does not exist**
  - `hunt_core/bootstrap.py:72 (and module docstring line 1)` · класс D / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** Line 1 docstring: 'Add monorepo root + hunt/ to sys.path'. Line 71-72 ImportError message: 'Install: pip install -e hunt/'. Grep confirms no `hunt/` package dir exists: `ls -d hunt/ hunt` -> 'No such file or directory'. The distributable package is `crypto-hunter` (pyproject.toml:6) and CLAUDE.md documents install as `uv sync --all-extras`. `pip install -e hunt/` would fail (no such path). Actual sys.path insertion (lines 37-41) adds the HUNTER repo root (`parents[1]`, misleadingly named `hunt_root`) and its parent (`repo`); neither is a `hunt/` subdir. So both the docstring and the user-facing remediation string describe a layout that no longer exists.
  - **Репро:** Trigger the ImportError branch: in an env missing e.g. polars_ta, run `python -c 'from hunt_core.bootstrap import require_feature_stack; require_feature_stack()'`. It advises `pip install -e hunt/`, which errors with 'Directory hunt/ is not installable' because no such directory exists; correct action is `uv sync --all-extras`.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Update the ImportError hint at line 71-72 from 'Install: pip install -e hunt/' to 'Install: uv sync --all-extras', and fix the module docstring at line 1 to say it adds the repo root (not a nonexistent `hunt/`). No logic change.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any Telegram signal text; this is a developer-facing startup error message only.

### data_readiness.py
- **Назначение:** Per-symbol data-readiness gate: checks frame history depth, mark price, spread, and live derivatives fields are fresh enough before a symbol is analyzed; also derives a graded 0-100 readiness score.
- **Методная опора:** No channel-method basis — infrastructure data-quality/freshness gate (Prizrak/Owner-of-Shorts/Spekulyantka say nothing about kline warmup or REST field readiness). Pure internal-consistency territory.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **composite_readiness_pct spread +10 is unreachable; score caps at 90, and 'spread present' scores the same as 'spread missing'**
  - `hunt_core/data_readiness.py:275 (producer gap at :200-208)` · класс C / calc / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** assess_symbol_data_readiness writes details['spread_bps'] ONLY inside the `if spread_bps is None:` branch (line 201: `details["spread_bps"] = None`). There is no else-branch that stores the actual value. So for every ready symbol with a valid spread, the key is simply absent from details. composite_readiness_pct line 275 reads `if details.get("spread_bps") is not None: score += 10.0` — get() returns None (key absent) whether the spread was valid or missing, so the +10 is never awarded. Recompute the reachable maximum: 4 frames x 20 (line 269) = 80, + spread 10 (unreachable) + derivatives 10 (line 277) = intended 100, but actual reachable max = 80 + 0 + 10 = 90. A fully-ready symbol with a good order book spread and a symbol where strict=False left spread missing both receive 0 spread points — the branch cannot distinguish them.
  - **Репро:** result = DataReadinessResult(ready=True, details={'frame_rows':{'5m':300,'15m':300,'1h':300,'4h':300}}); composite_readiness_pct(result) returns 90, not 100 — even though this mirrors a symbol whose spread_bps was a valid finite value (which is never recorded in details). Add an assert composite_readiness_pct(...)==100 for a fully-ready symbol and it fails at 90.
  - **Мин. фикс:** In assess_symbol_data_readiness add an else that records the real value: `if spread_bps is None: details['spread_bps']=None; ... else: details['spread_bps']=float(spread_bps)`. No new data/deps — spread_bps is already fetched at line 200.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None today (see orphan finding — composite_pct is not rendered). If composite_pct is ever surfaced to TG as the docstring promises, the '0-100 data readiness' number would rise from a 90 ceiling to a true 100 for clean symbols and would finally reflect whether spread data is present.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **composite_pct is an orphan output — produced and stored in the row dict but read by nobody; docstring claims it is 'for TG'**
  - `hunt_core/data_readiness.py:282-286 (readiness_dict_for_row) / consumed at hunt_core/runtime/tick_assembly.py:1151` · класс D / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** grep -rn 'composite_pct' over the whole repo (*.py, docs) returns exactly two hits: the definition in data_readiness.py:285 and nothing else. readiness_dict_for_row is called only at tick_assembly.py:1151 which writes result['data_readiness'] = {'ready':..., 'composite_pct':...}; grep for readers of the 'composite_pct' key (and of 'data_readiness' downstream) shows the only downstream reader is tests/test_universe_health.py which reads {'data_readiness':{'ready':True}} — never composite_pct. No deliver/telegram/render module reads it. The docstring at line 262 says 'Graded 0-100 data readiness for TG (P0-D)' but it is never rendered into any Telegram text.
  - **Репро:** grep -rn '"composite_pct"\|composite_pct' . --include='*.py' -> only hunt_core/data_readiness.py:285. No consumer.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either wire composite_pct into the setup/no-signal Telegram line (deliver) if the 0-100 grade is wanted, or drop composite_readiness_pct + readiness_dict_for_row's composite_pct entry as dead output. Prefer deletion unless a TG surface is intended.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** No change to any signal today; the value is computed and thrown away. Deleting it removes a misleading 'for TG' claim; wiring it would add a readiness % to the no-signal/setup line.

### secrets.py
- **Назначение:** Loads Telegram bot token / chat ids / operator user-ids from .env + environment (canonical keys with legacy aliases) into a frozen Secrets value.
- **Методная опора:** No method basis — pure infrastructure/config plumbing for the Telegram delivery layer; not a signal feature.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Secrets.lab_chat_id is an orphan field — produced, read by nobody**
  - `hunt_core/secrets.py:20,100,105` · класс C / dead-code / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** load_secrets() resolves lab_chat_id (line 100: `_first_configured_env("TELEGRAM_LAB_CHAT_ID","HUNT_LAB_CHAT_ID")`) and stores it on Secrets (line 105). Grep for the consumer: `grep -rn "\.lab_chat_id" --include=*.py .` returns ZERO reads of the attribute anywhere in the repo. The only actual lab-chat consumer, hunt_core/deliver/lab.py:8-12 `lab_chat_id()`, re-reads os.environ directly (`os.environ.get("TELEGRAM_LAB_CHAT_ID")` / `HUNT_LAB_CHAT_ID`) and never touches Secrets. domain/config.py load_settings (lines 271-273) forwards secrets.tg_token/target_chat_id/operator_user_ids into the payload but deliberately omits secrets.lab_chat_id, so it never reaches HuntSettings either. The env-var side effect of load_dotenv() (inside load_secrets) is what actually feeds lab.py; the Secrets.lab_chat_id field itself is inert.
  - **Репро:** Set TELEGRAM_LAB_CHAT_ID in .env, call load_secrets(); s.lab_chat_id is populated but no code path ever consumes s.lab_chat_id (grep proves it). Lab routing works only because load_dotenv populated os.environ, not because of this field.
  - **Мин. фикс:** Either forward it — add `payload["lab_chat_id"] = secrets.lab_chat_id` in config.py load_settings and have deliver/lab.py read settings.lab_chat_id — or drop the field and its resolution (lines 20, 100, 105) since lab.py already reads env directly. No signal/data change either way.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None. Telegram signal text is unchanged; this is dead plumbing.
- ⏸ *не верифицировано (session limit)* — **Secrets is a frozen dataclass where the charter mandates a Pydantic BaseModel value-model**
  - `hunt_core/secrets.py:16-21` · класс C / library / **P2**
  - **Доказательство:** CLAUDE.md key rules: "Pydantic BaseModel for domain models — no dataclasses". Round-1 G-26 already converted dataclass→Pydantic across the codebase; the session carve-out lists ManipulationSetup/PrescanEngine/_DebouncedSymbol as deliberate dataclasses BECAUSE they need mutation. Secrets (lines 16-21) is `@dataclass(frozen=True)` — an immutable value-model with no mutation need, i.e. exactly the case the Pydantic rule targets, and it is NOT in the deliberate-dataclass carve-out. The sibling config value model HuntSettings (domain/config.py:120) is a Pydantic model, so this is an internal inconsistency, not a deliberate exception.
  - **Репро:** Static/charter check: this frozen value-model is a dataclass while its peer HuntSettings is Pydantic; no field validation (e.g. token/chat-id are unvalidated raw strings that a BaseModel could coerce/validate).
  - **Мин. фикс:** Convert Secrets to a frozen Pydantic BaseModel (model_config frozen=True), keeping the same fields/defaults; no data or signal change.
  - **Сигнал before/after:** None. Internal type-hygiene only; no change to any delivered message.
